USA_american_civil_war = {


	USA_retake_control_over_STATE = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			is_USA_civil_war_tag = yes
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = USA_american_cw
			FROM = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
			} 
		}
		state_target = yes
		cost = 20
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = original_US_core
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 90000
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 35

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	USA_global_offensive_against_TAG = {
		visible = {

			}
		}
		targeted_modifier = {
			tag = FROM
			attack_bonus_against = 0.7
		}
		days_remove = 120
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = offensive_underway
				days = 120
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

USA_ruin_everything = {

	USA_civil_war_time = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = usa_civil_war_prevented }
			OR = {
				country_exists = CSA
			}
		}

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = usa_its_time
		}

		complete_effect = {
			#country_event = { id = usa.1859 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	USA_release_the_CSA = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {

war_measures = {

	USA_meeting_with_einstein = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			has_civil_war = no
			has_war = no
		}

		cost = 150
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}

		visible = {
			GER = { has_tech = atomic_research }
		}

		complete_effect = {

		}
	}

	USA_homeland_defense = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = USA
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = USA
				}
			}
			has_civil_war = no
		}

		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}

		visible = {
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_support > 0.89 }
				}
				set_war_support = 0.9
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = great_depression
				}
				remove_ideas = great_depression
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = extensive_conscription
							has_idea = scraping_the_barrel
							has_idea = service_by_requirement
							has_idea = all_adults_serve
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = extensive_conscription
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = undisturbed_isolation
						has_idea = isolation
						has_idea = civilian_economy
						has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
					}
				}
				add_ideas = war_economy
			}
			add_ideas = USA_homeland_defense
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -3 }
			}
		}

	USA_mexican_intervention = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				MEX = { has_government = fascism }
				MEX = { has_government = communism }
				MEX = { fascism > 0.4 }
				MEX = { communism > 0.4 }
			}
		}

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				AND = {
					NOT = { MEX = { has_government = fascism } }
					NOT = { MEX = { has_government = communism } }
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_government = democratic
		}

		complete_effect = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				target = MEX
			}
		}

	}

	USA_deploy_national_guard = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}

		available = {
			has_civil_war = no
			OR = {
				has_war = yes
				threat > 0.99
			}
		}

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}

		visible = {
			always = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_support } }
				set_technology = { tech_support = 1 }
			}
			USA = { load_oob = "USA_national_guard" }
			set_country_flag = USA_already_deployed_troops
		}
	}

					modules = {
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_1 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_2 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
						fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
						fixed_ship_engine_slot = carrier_ship_engine_2
						fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_ship_secondaries
						front_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
						#mid_2_custom_slot = ship_deck_space

					}
					obsolete = yes
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1
						creator = "USA"
						version_name = "Ranger Class"
					}
					name = "USS Ranger"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.99
					amount = 1
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Yorktown Class"
					type = ship_hull_carrier_1
					name_group = USA_CV_HISTORICAL
					parent_version = 0
					modules = {
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_1 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_deck_slot_2 = ship_deck_space
						fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2

						fixed_ship_engine_slot = carrier_ship_engine_2

						front_1_custom_slot = ship_deck_space
						#mid_2_custom_slot = ship_deck_space

					}
					#obsolete = yes
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1
						creator = "USA"
						version_name = "Yorktown Class"
					}
					name = "USS Yorktown"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.93
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1
						creator = "USA"
						version_name = "Yorktown Class"
					}
					name = "USS Enterprise"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.3
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ship_hull_carrier_1
						creator = "USA"
						version_name = "Yorktown Class"
					}
					name = "USS Wasp"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.01
					amount = 1
				}

				else = {
					set_technology = { basic_carrier = 1 }
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Yorktown class"
						type = carrier_2
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 2

						}
					}
					add_equipment_production = {

							version_name = "Yorktown Class"
						}
						name = "USS Yorktown"

USA_canadian_issue = {

	USA_annex_canada = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = USA
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_civil_war = no
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CAN }
				CAN = { is_subject_of = ENG }
			}
			NOT = {
				ROOT = {
					owns_state = 276
					owns_state = 468
					owns_state = 465
					owns_state = 464
					owns_state = 466
					owns_state = 682
					owns_state = 683
					owns_state = 467
					owns_state = 469
					owns_state = 472
					owns_state = 470
					owns_state = 473
					owns_state = 471
					owns_state = 740
					owns_state = 739
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_Secure_Canada
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				transfer_state = 276
				transfer_state = 468
				transfer_state = 465
				transfer_state = 464
				transfer_state = 466
				transfer_state = 682
				transfer_state = 683
				transfer_state = 467
				transfer_state = 469
				transfer_state = 472
				transfer_state = 470
				transfer_state = 473
				transfer_state = 471
				transfer_state = 740
				transfer_state = 739

			}
		}
	}

	USA_join_the_united_states = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = CAN
		}

		available = {
			has_government = democratic
		}

		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_Secure_Canada
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_Secure_Canada } }

				USA = { annex_country = { target = CAN } }
			}
		}
	}

USA_trade_embargo = {

	USA_trade_embargo_against_japan = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = USA
				original_tag = FRA
				original_tag = ENG
				original_tag = SOV
				original_tag = HOL
				original_tag = FRA
			}
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
		}

		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}

		visible = {
			USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_Embargo_Japan }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo }

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = ENG
					MAL = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
				MAL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = ENG
					RAJ = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
				RAJ = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = ENG
					SAF = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
				SAF = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = HOL
					INS = { is_subject_of = HOL } }
				INS = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo } }
			}

		}
	}

USA_instigate_communist_uprisings_category = {

	USA_instigate_communist_uprisings = {
	
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		days_remove = 30

		allowed = {
			original_tag = USA
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_send_covert_agents
		}
		
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_send_covert_agents
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					capital_scope = {
						is_on_continent = south_america
					}
					AND = {
						capital_scope = {
							is_on_continent = north_america
						}
						NOT = {
							original_tag = USA
						}	
					}
				}	
				NOT = {
					OR = {
					has_government = communism
					tag = XXB
				}
				}
			}
        }

		available = {
			FROM = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_subject = no
				communism > 0.15
			}
		}

		cost = 75
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						num_of_controlled_states < 2	
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_financed
							has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_armed
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					random_list = {
    					75 = {
       						country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1505
    					}
						25 = {
							country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1507
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						num_of_controlled_states < 2	
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_financed
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_armed
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					random_list = {
    					33 = {
       						country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1505
    					}
						66 = {
							country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1507
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						num_of_controlled_states > 1
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_financed
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_armed
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_financed
							has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_armed
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					random_list = {
    					50 = {
       						country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1506
    					}
						50 = {
							country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1507
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						num_of_controlled_states > 1	
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_financed
						has_country_flag = USAAH_revolutionaries_armed
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					random_list = {
    					33 = {
       						country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1506
    					}
						66 = {
							country_event = RON_American_Alt_History.1507
						}
					}	
				}	
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

CAN_independence_struggle_category_usa = {

	CAN_spread_independentist_sentiments_usa = {

		icon = eng_trade_unions_demand
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_invite_communists_central_america
		}
		available = {
			tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_help_canada
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAN_canadian_independence_settled
			}
			CAN = {
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			NOT = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = CAN_not_demand_referendum_usa_tt	
					check_variable = { var = ENG.eng_can_loyalist_influence value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }	
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAN_canadian_independence_settled
			}
		}

		targets = { CAN }

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = CAN
			}
		}

		days_remove = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CAN = {
					check_variable = { var = ENG.eng_can_loyalist_influence value = 20 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					check_variable = { var = eng_temp_can_influence value = 10 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = -100
				has_political_power < 0
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						CAN = {
							has_country_flag = CAN_favoured_britain
						}
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CAN = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_favoured_britain
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -75
			}	
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = usa_can_independence_influence value = 5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_spread_independentist_sentiments_usa_tt
			CAN = {
				set_variable = { var = usa_temp_can_influence value = USA.usa_can_independence_influence }
				subtract_from_variable = { var = usa_temp_can_influence value = ENG.eng_can_loyalist_influence }
				set_variable = { var = eng_temp_can_influence value = ENG.eng_can_loyalist_influence }
				subtract_from_variable = { var = eng_temp_can_influence value = USA.usa_can_independence_influence }
			}
		}
	}

	CAN_demand_referendum_usa = {

		icon = eng_trade_unions_demand
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_invite_communists_central_america
		}

		available = {
			tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USAAH_help_canada
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAN_canadian_independence_settled
			}
			CAN = {
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
   				tooltip = CAN_demand_referendum_usa_tt	
				check_variable = { var = USA.usa_can_independence_influence value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }	
    		}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAN_canadian_independence_settled
			}
		}

		targets = { CAN }

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = CAN
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
				modifier = {
				factor = -100
				has_political_power < 0
			}
